1b1(phal chen): dam pa brgya rtse gsum pa/ de nas tshang dpon gyi du nor bdangs rgya
1b2(phal chen): sems dpa' rnam par thar pa sgra yid du 'ong ba dang / rnam par 'phrul pa bang mo la 'jug pa de da
1b3(phal chen): kyang rgya cher bsgom pa dang / yid ches par bya ba dang / shin tu rgyas par byed cing / mtshan
1b4(phal chen): mo'i lha mo shing thams cad kyi me tog rgyas pas bde bar gnas pa gang na ba der phyin nas/ mtshan
2a1(phal chen): #/ mo'i lha mo shing thams cad kyi me tog rgyas pas bde bar gnas pa spos rin po che thams
2a2(phal chen): cad kyi shing gi yal ga'i khang pa brtsegs bzhig na seng ge'i khri rin po che'i shing gi myu gu'i snying po can zhig la
2a3(phal chen): 'dug ste/ mtshan mo'i lha mo stong phrag bcus kun nas bskor cing 'dug pa mthong ngo // de nas tshang dpon
2a4(phal chen): gyi bu nor bzangs kyis mtshan mo'i lha mo shing thams cad kyi me tog rgyas pas bde bar gnas pa'i rkang pa gnyis
2b1(phal chen): laskyo bos phyag 'tshal te/ mdun du 'dug nas/ zil mo sbyar te 'di skad ces smras so// lha mo bdag gis zlan phre
2b2(phal chen): ba yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed na/ ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' rnams/ byang chub sem
2b3(phal chen): dpa'i spyad pa spyod pa dang / ji ltar spyod ji ltar slob cing thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du 'byung ba bdag la bshad du gso
2b4(phal chen): de skad ces smras pa dang / mtshan mo'i lha mo shing thams cad kyi me tog rgyas pas bde bar gnas pas/ tshong dpon gyi du
2b5(phal chen): nor bzangs la 'di skad ces smras so// rigs kyi bu kho mo'i mthus ni mi mjed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na nyi ma nub tu cha
3a1(phal chen): ba'i tshe/ pad mo shin tu rgyas pa'i rnams kyang rnam par 'dzum par 'gyur ro//
3a2(phal chen): skyes pa dang / bud med 'aza' shing gi ra ban gnas shing dga' bar rtse ba brtson pa dag kyang khyim du 'dod pa'irma
3a3(phal chen): skyed do// lam dang srang na rgyu ba'i sems can rnams kyang zhag gi gnas sems shing 'chol te/ 'gro
3a4(phal chen): ba'i gnas thams cad du mngon par gzhol bar 'gyur ro// nags tshal dang / gse ba dang / bug la
3a5(phal chen): rten pa'i sems can rnams kyang nags tshal dang / gseb dang / phug du 'dong ngo // shing la gnas pa'i
3b1(phal chen): masacan namasang gi gnas la chen par mngon par man ma // da nA gnas pa'i sems canan smra
3b2(phal chen): // zung dang / grong khyer dang / ljongs dang / yul la gnas pa'i sems can mas kyang nga
3b3(phal chen): khyer dang yul du 'dong ngo // chun gnas pa'i sems can rnams kyang chur 'dong ngo // thogs gzhan gyi yul du phyin
3b4(phal chen): ba'i sems can rnams kyang nub mo 'a zhing dga' bar gnas pa don du rang rang gi yul gyi phyogs kyi bsam pa
3b5(phal chen): bskyed do// rigs kyi bu gzhan yang kho ni skyes pa dang / bud med gzhon nu da ral dang
3b6(phal chen): ba dar ba'i nyams drod kyi nyos pa/ glu dang gar dang / rol mo'i dga' bas myos pa dang
4a1(phal chen): 'dod pa'i yon tan la dga' zhing brtson pa rnams le skye ba dang / rga shi dang / gti mug gi mun pa chen pos 'jigs pa'i gnyen por
4a2(phal chen): dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su bskyed pa'i phyir brtson 'grus kyis legs par bsngags par byed do// sems can ser sna dang ldan pa rnams ni sbyin pa la rab tu sbyor ro//
4a3(phal chen): sems can tshul khrims ngan pa can rnams ni tshul khrims la rab tu 'god do// ngan sems dang ldan pa'i sems can rnams la ni byams pa'i legs pa brjod do//
4a4(phal chen): sems 'khrugs pa'i sems can rnams ni bzod pa la rab tu 'god do// le lo can gyi sems can rnams ni byang chub sems dpa'i brtson 'grus brtsam pa la rab tu
4a5(phal chen): 'god do// sems rnam par myos pa'i sems can rnams ni bsam gtan la rab tu 'god do// shes rab 'tshal pa can gyi sems can rnams ni shes rab kyi
4a6(phal chen): pha rol tu phyin pa la yongs su sbyor ro// theg pa dma' ba la mos pa'i sems can rnams ni theg pa chen po la rab tu 'god do// khams gsum la mngon par
4a7(phal chen): zhen pa'i sems can rnams ni byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam gyi pha rol tu phyin pa srid pa lam gyi rgyud mthar phyin pa'i dkyil 'khor la spyod pa la rab tu 'gad
4a8(phal chen): dmigs pa'i dbang du gyur pa'i sems can las dang nyon mongs pos rab tu mnar ba/ jisod nams dang ye shes kyi stobs med pa rnams ni/
4b1(phal chen): chubs mapas pa gyur pa/ sa pa na nag gyis bas pa smra sa na ngas sun padang /
4b2(phal chen): kun gnag tu 'joms pan smras ni/ byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes kyi phyi rol tu phyin pa la rab tu 'gad do// rigs kyi su gzhan yang la'i byung chum sems da
4b3(phal chen): rnam par thar pa dga' ba'i 'od smrab yongs pa yang dag par 'byung bathob bo// nor b.rangs kyis smras pa/ lha ma byung chub sems dpa'i rnam pa bar blta rlo
4b4(phal chen): smra ba yangs pa yang dag par 'byung ba de'i yul ji lta bu ni ga mchis/ smras pa rigs kyi bu rnam par thar pa de ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i bsod napas kyis
4b5(phal chen): can yongs su sdud pa'i ye shes dang / thabs snang ba dang ldan pa ste/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ rigs kyi bu sems can rnams kyi bde ba nyams su myong ba ji skyed
4b6(phal chen): cig yod pa de dag thams cad ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i bsod nams kyi mthus byung ba'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdams ngag gi tshul gyis byung ba ma/
4b7(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung la nan tan du byas pas byung ba'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i rjes su bslabs pas byung ba'o// de bzhin gshegs pa
4b8(phal chen): snyan pa'i lam la nan tan du byas pas byung ba'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyi brlabs kyis byung ba'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i snyan pa'i lam la nan
5a1(phal chen): tu byas pas byung ba'o// de bzhin gshegs pa dang tshul 'dra ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pas byung ba'o// de bzhin gshegs pas chos bstan
5a2(phal chen): pa'i 'thun pa'i rgyus byung ba'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi nyi ma snang bas byung ba'o// rigs kyi bu de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi chos dkar po'i
5a3(phal chen): dkyil 'khor gyi snang bas ni sems can rnams kyi snang bas ni sems can rnams kyi bde ba yongs su 'byung ba ste/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar rigs kyi bu tham
5a4(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa dga' ba'i 'od spro ba yangs pa yang dag par 'byung ba 'di la 'jug pa'i tshe/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa
5a5(phal chen): dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnam par snang mdzad kyi sngon gyi byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rgya mtsho rjes su dran par byed cing / 'jug pa
5a6(phal chen): dang / khong du chud par byed pa'i tshe/ 'di ltar bcom ldan 'das sngon byang chub sems dpa'i sa la bzhugs pas/ sems can bdag tu bya ba dang / byangag
5a7(phal chen): gir bya ba la mngon par zhen pa/ ma rig pa'i mun pas 'joms pa/ lta ba thibs po'i bras mtha' dgon par 'khyams pa/ sred pa'i dbang du gyur pa/ 'dod chag/
5a8(phal chen): kyi bcing bas glags pa/ zhe sdang gi khong khro ba'i sems dang ldan pa/ gti mug gi sems kyi rgyud 'khrugs par gyur pa/ thag dog dang sor skas kun nas
5b1(phal chen): 'khor pa/ nyon mongs pas rab tu dgrags pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal chen po nyams su myong bar gyur pa/ 'khor bran phongs pa'i
5b2(phal chen): sdug bsngal gyis rab tu garI ra bya/ sangs rgyas blta ba las phyir phyogs par gyur pa thams cad gzigs nas thugs rje chen po'i thugs skyes par gyur
5b3(phal chen): sems can thams cad kyi don du 'gro ba thams cad la yo byad dang / rin po ches yongs su bsdu zhing yongs su sdud pa'i thugs dang / sems can thams
5b4(phal chen): cad kyi 'khor ba'i yo byad yongs su bslab pa'i thugs dang / dngos po thams cad la chags mi mnga' ba'i thugs dang / yul thams cad la ye bajam pa
5b5(phal chen): mi mnga' ba'i thugs dang / dka' ba thams cad la chags pa mi mnga' ba'i thugs dang / longs spyod thams cad la yongs su mazhen pa'i thugs dang /
5b6(phal chen): spyan thams cad la yongs su rnam par smin pa la re ba med pa'i thugs dang / 'jig rten phun sum tshogs pa thams cad la bzhed pa mi mnga' ba'i
5b7(phal chen): thugs dang / rgyu dang rkyen la marmongs pa'i thugs dang / legs par bcal ba'i chos la yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du mkhyen pa'i thugs dang / sems
5b8(phal chen): can thams cad kyi don la gzhol bar bya ba mngon par bsgrub pa'i thugs kyang skye bar 'gyur te/ de de ltar chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin la yang dag
6a1(phal chen): par zhugs pa'i thugs dang ldan pa/ sems can gyi khams thams cad du byams pa chen pos snyoms par zhugs pa/ 'gro ba
6a2(phal chen): thams cad thugs rje chen po'i sprin gyis rgyas par dgang ba'i sbyor ba mnga' ba/ sems can gyi 'jig rten thams cad kun nas khebs pa'i chos kyi gdugs
6a3(phal chen): chen po'i dkyil 'khor mnga' ba/ sems can thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa'i rnam par 'joms pa'i ye shes rdo rje'i mtshon cha mnga' ba/ 'gro ba thams cad
6a4(phal chen): kyi bde ba yongs su bsgrubs pas/ dgyes pa'i shugs rnam par 'phel ba'i thugs mnga' ba/ sems can thams cad la bde ba phul du phyin pa mngon par
6a5(phal chen): bsgrub pa'i smon lam gyi thugs mnga' ba/ bsam pa dang smon pa ji lta ba bzhin du sems can thams cad la nor gyi char rab tu dbab pa'i thugs mnga' ba/ sems
6a6(phal chen): can thams cad yongs su mi btang zhing snyoms par sbyor ba'i thugs mnga' ba/ 'phags pa'i non gyis sems can thams cad tshim par mdzad pa'i thugs mnga'
6a7(phal chen): ba/ stobs bcu'i ye shes rin po che phul du dri ma med pa thob par mdzad pa'i thugs mnga' ba/ byang chub sems dpa'i mngon par shes pa chen po'i stobs dang
6a8(phal chen): shugs rab tu brnyes pa de/ byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par 'phrul pa sna tshogs kyi sprin chen pos sems can gyi khams kyi chos kyi dbyings kyis klas pa/
6b1(phal chen): nam ma pa'i rnams gtugs pa thams cad rgyas par dkar ste/ sems can thams cad la mdun par gyur bar zhugs shing sbyin pa'i dmigs pa thams cad kyi nga
6b2(phal chen): myi char chen po rnam pa thams cad du dbab pa dang / rin po che'i rgyan thams cad kyi sprin chen po'i char mngon par 'bebs par mdzad de/ 'di ltar sem
6b3(phal chen): thams cadas so'i tshul dang / ji ltar 'thun pas longs spyod par bya ba'i phyir dngos po rnam pa tha dad pa mtha' yas pa yongs su btang ba dang / yo zung rnam pa
6b4(phal chen): tha dad tshad med pa la spyad par bya ba dang / sbyin pa rnam pa sna tshogs thams cad kyis yongs su bsdu ba'i tshul dang / dngos po yongs su gtang ba rnam pa du ma
6b5(phal chen): la yongs su spyad pa dang / yo byad kyi rnam pa dang / rgyan gyi 'du byed brjod du med pa dang / sbyin pa'i tshogs rnam pa sna tshogs mtshan nyid sna tshogs dang ldan
6b6(phal chen): pa'i sems can rnams bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su tshim par bya bar mngon par bsgrubs po'i dngos po thams cad btang ba dang / yongs su btang ba dang /
6b7(phal chen): sbyin par btang ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal rgyun mi 'chad pa las yongs su sgrub pa'i tshul du bya ba rnams/ sems can thams cad la lan
6b8(phal chen): rab mi mnga' ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad la mnyam pa nyid du byung ba'i thugs mnga' ba/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi sems rin po che yongs su sbyong ba mdzad cing / sangs
7a1(phal chen): rgyas thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba rgya mtsho gcig tu gyur pa las byung ba'i yongs su bsdu ba'i tshul 'gro ba thams cad kyi bsam pa ji lta
7a2(phal chen): ba bzhin du yo byad kyi char dbab pa/ 'gro ba thams cad la thams cad mkhyen pa'i bsod nams rgya mtsho'i shugs rnam par 'phel bar mdzad pas thugs kyi skad
7a3(phal chen): cig re re la/ sems can ma lus pa thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba dang / gdul ba gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir mngon
7a4(phal chen): par sgrub pa mdzad pa dang / thugs kyi skad cig re re li zhing gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa ma lus pa thams cad sangs rgyas kyi zhing nye bar nyon mongs pa med
7a5(phal chen): cing bla na med pa'i rgyan rnam par dag pas rnam par grub cing / rab tu brgyan pa yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang / thugs kyi skad cig re re la chos kyi chu
7a6(phal chen): rgya mtsho ma lus par thams cad rgyas par dgang ba rnam par dag par bya ba dang / thugs kyi skad cig re re la nam mkha'i dbyings kyi gtos ma lus pa thams
7a7(phal chen): cad rgyas par dgang ba'i ye shes kyi tshul yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang / thugs kyi skad cig re re la sems can dang dus ma lus pa thams cad la 'a
7a8(phal chen): pa'i ye shes kyi tshul rnam par dag par bya ba dang / thugs kyi skad cig re re la 'gro ba ma lus pa thams cad rnam par 'dul ba'i ye shes kyi tshul snang
7b1(phal chen): sgru par bya ba dang / thugs snga ma cig rnamal dus sa lus pa thams cad du mas kyi 'khar sa bskor ba las phyir mi ldog par bya ba dang / thugs can
7b2(phal chen): cig ri rnal thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi byin gyi rlabs la mkhas pa ma lus par yongs su brgyan dus/ 'gro ba thams cad la phan 'dugs par gyur
7b3(phal chen): thugs kyi skad cig re re la 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa'i grangs su bya ba'i rgyud dang ldan pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad mngon par 'dzin du/
7b4(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad yongs su 'du ba/ 'jig rten gyi khams 'jam klas pa sna tshogs brjod du yod pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyu
7b5(phal chen): rnam par gnas pa sna tshogs kyis mtshams rnam par brgyan pa gni sna tshogs dang lhun du mar brjod du yod pa/ rnam par phye ba sna tshogs kyi skal ba rnam
7b6(phal chen): pa tha dad pa bstan du yod pa/ kun nas nyon mongs shing rnam par dag pa dang / rnam par dag cing kun nas nyon mongs pa dang / gcig tu yongs su dag pa
7b7(phal chen): dang / gcig tu kun nas nyon mongs pa dang / che ba dang / yangs pa dang / tshad med pa dang / dog pa dang / phra ba dang / rgya che ba dang / gzhi mnyam pa
7b8(phal chen): dang snrel zhi dang / spyi'u tshugs dang / phyogs dang phyogs mtshams su mngon par ltas pa dang / phyogs rgya mtsho sna tshogs su gzhol ba/ sgo sna
8a1(phal chen): tshogs nas bstan cing sgo mtha' yas pa'i dbyibs rnam pa sna tshogs su 'dug pa'i rnam par phye ba sna tshogs dang ldan pa'i 'jig
8a2(phal chen): rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad du byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa spyad de/ byang chub sems dpa'i skyon med pa yongs su mnan nas byang chub sems dpa'i
8a3(phal chen): spyod pa dang / rnam par 'phrul pas rgyas par dgang bar bya ba dang / thugs kyi skad cig re re la dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las ma lus pa thams
8a4(phal chen): cad sems can pha rol gyi sems dang / bsam pas rnam par dmigs par bya ba'i phyir 'gro ba thams cad la thams cad mkhyen pa'i bsod nams rgya mtshor
8a5(phal chen): shugs rnam par 'phel bar mdzad de/ mngon par bsgrub pa mdzad par gyur pa mngon par shes so// rjes su dran no// rigs kyi bu de ltar bcom ldan
8a6(phal chen): 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad sngon byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa mdzad pa'i tshe/ 'jig rten gnas pa bsod nams dang ye shes kyi
8a7(phal chen): tshogs dang bral ba/ sems can byas pa drin du mo gzo bas yongs su gang ba/ mi shes pa'i mun pas chod pa// badrug gir bya ba la mngon par zhen pa/
8a8(phal chen): ma rig pa'i mun pa dang rab rib kyis sgribs pa/ tshul bzhin ma yin par rnam par rtog pa la zhugs pa thibs po'i bas mtha' dgon par mgo rlag pa

8b2(phal chen): srog bcul sna tshogs rnams su zang bar gyur pa rnams la thugs rje chen po bskyed de/ pha rol tu phyin pa skyed pa'i sprin rgya chen po mngon par bsgru
8b3(phal chen): dge ba'i rtsa ba la brtan par gnas pa yongs su bsngags pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi 'khor ba'i phongs pa'i sdug bsngal rnam par bzlog pa dang /
8b4(phal chen): bsod nams dang ye shes kyi chags chen po la mngon par mos par bya ba dang / rgyu ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi phyogs mngon par bstan pa dang / las deng chos su

10a3(phal chen): sems dang / bdud kyi 'khor dang / nyon mongs pa thams cad kyis mi thub pa'i sems dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi ye shes thob par bya bar skabs bye
10a4(phal chen): ba'i sems kyis khong du chud pa dang / 'jug pa dang / yid ches par bya ba dang / gzung ba dang / rjes su 'brang bar bya ba dang / shes par bya bar nus so//
10a5(phal chen): de ci'i phyir zhe na/ rigs kyi bu gnas 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi yul te/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyis kyang yongs su mnor na/
10a6(phal chen): sems can gzhan thams cad kyis lta ci zhig smos/ 'on kyang sems can cang shes rnams kyi bsam pa phun sum tshogs pa rnam par dag par bya ba dang / dge
10a7(phal chen): ba'i rtsa ba la spyod pa'i sems can rnams kyi lhag pa'i bsam pa dbang du 'gyur bar bya ba dang / khyod kyis bsam pa thag pa nas yongs su dris pa'i lung bsnun
10a8(phal chen): pa'i chos nyid rab tu byung ba thob par bya ba'i phyir de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis rlabs kyis bstan to// de nas mtshan mo'i lha mo shing thams cad kyi me tog
10b1(phal chen): sa na
10b2(phal chen): nga rnams na / mas sa na ma na
10b3(phal chen): ma na ni / sems sna rdzun pa du/ na sa /
10b4(phal chen): da gas pas bsas sas gyur ban/ ma ma nyid shes swA~M / 'gi ga 'ang gi sa /
10b5(phal chen): rgyus bsam pa rnogs par gyur pa dang // nyon mongs las kyi sgrib pas bsgribs pa yis// spangs rgyas yul 'di shes par mi nus so//
10b6(phal chen): khams dang skye mched gnas pa dang // 'jig tshogs mang la gnas par gyur pa dang // lha sems 'du 'du shes byin ci log gyur pas/
10b7(phal chen): sa 'di shes par mi nus so// rgyal ba'i yul ni shes dka' ni ba ste// rang bzhin dri med rnam par rtog pa medo// srid par rten cing 'khor la cha
10b8(phal chen): pa yis// chos 'di yang dag shes par mi nus so// sangs rgyas rigs su rigs ldan gang skyes pa// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyis byin rlabs zhe/
11a1(phal chen): chos kyi rgyal po'i gdung rabs yongs 'dzin pa// drang srong de dag yul ni 'di yin no// dkar chos rgya mtshos mi ngoms sems ldan ning //
11a2(phal chen): gang rnams dge ba'i bshes kyis yongs bzung ste// thub pa'i stobs la dmigs pa'i sems sprin can// de dag 'di thos bzod pa thob par 'gyur// gang rnams
11a3(phal chen): bsams pa dri med rnam rtog med// bar snang mkha' bzhin phyogs dang phyogs mtshams su// mur pa rnam bsngal blo gros sgron ma'i snyir// dri med de dag spyong yul 'di yin//
11a4(phal chen): snying rje'i bsam pas 'gro ba'i rgya mtsho rnams// dus gsum byung ba gang rnams rgyas byed cing // sems can ma lus rjes 'brang byams pa can// de dag rgyal ba'i tshul
11a5(phal chen): 'dir 'jug par 'gyur// gang rnams 'dzin med dga' ba'i sems ldan zhing // rtag par bdog pa thams cad sbyin bcol la// sems can kun la mnyam par zhugs gyur pa/
11a6(phal chen): chags med dge sbyong yul 'di yin// nyon mongs med sems skyon me skyong ldan zhing // gang rnabs 'gyod pa rnam bsal sems ldan te// sangs rgyas gdams ngag nan
11a7(phal chen): tan byed ldar ba// dri med de dag spyod yul 'di yin no// gang rnams mi bskul sems ldan mi skyod sems// chos kyi rang bzhin rtogs pa'i sems ldan zhing //
11a8(phal chen): kyi rgya mtshor mi 'gal sems ldan pa// mi zad de dag rnam thar 'di yin no// gang rnams mi sgo'i sems dang mi ldog sems// brjod 'grus mthu dang stsal du ldan padas/
11b1(phal chen): thams cad mthad tshogs brtson 'grus mtha' yas pa// brtul zhugs bzang ldar de dag yul 'di yin// zhi ba'i sems ldan mnyam par gzhag bgang // shin du'i rba
11b2(phal chen): rims nga thal ba rnams// kun mkhyen pasam gtam ldan 'ag mtshod sbyang ba// rab tu'i pade dag rgyal 'di yin// gang rnams chags bkun las sems sa da
11b3(phal chen): chos kyi rang bzhin khong du chud sems can// rgyal ba'i chos dbyings rtogs par khong chung ba// shes rab skor ma de dag tshul 'di yid// sems can rang bzhin rtog se/
11b4(phal chen): ldan gyur cing // gang rnams sring ba'i mchol chags med sems// sems can sems la gzugs brnyan zla 'char ba// lam mkhan de dag rnamathar 'di yin no// dus
11b5(phal chen): gsum byung ba'i rgyal ba rgya mtsho rnams// smon lam gang chen mtsho'i rgyud skyes pa'i// zhing rnams kun du phyi ma'i mthar skyong ba// kun du bzang po de dag tshul 'di yin/
11b6(phal chen): gang rnams chos dbyings tshul rnams rgya mtsho yas// 'gro ba rgya mtsho 'du dang 'jig pa yi// bsal par bcas pa khong du chung ba rnams// rtog med de dag rnam thar 'di sa
11b7(phal chen): no// zhing rnams kun gyi rdul phran thams cad la// sangs rgyas grangs med shing rgyal drung bzhugs shing // byang chub 'chang rgya 'gro 'dul mthong ba yi// rags med
11b8(phal chen): mig can de dag tshul 'di yin// khyod ni sal ba rgya mtsho rgya chen du// dge ba'i bzhes gnyen mang po bsnyen bskur te// chos 'dod chos tshol mi skyo 'dir dbyibs
12a1(phal chen): thos nas de ni yongs su gzung bar nus// khyod kyi bsam pa yongs su sbyang ba'i phyir// bde gshegs byin brlabs bsam gyis khyab pas/
12a2(phal chen): rnam par snang mdzad tshad med yul 'di yang // kho mo'i tshig las chags pa med par 'byung // rigs kyi bu sngon 'das pa'i dus bskal ba 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul shin du dra ba snyed
12a3(phal chen): kyi pha rol de'i yang pha snga zhig tu 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho gser rin po che'i ri spos rnam par snang ba zhes bya ba byung ste/ rigs kyi bu 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho gser rin po che'i ma
12a4(phal chen): rnam par snang ba der de bzhin gshegs pa ye shes ri bo'i 'od chos kyi dbyings su snang ba'i gzi brjid rgyal po zhes bya ba byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa ye shes kyi ri bo'i 'od chos
12a5(phal chen): kyi dbyings su snang ba'i gzi brjid rgyal po de sngon byang chub sems dpa'i sbyong ba mdzad pa'i tshe// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho ga ser rin po che'i ri sngo rnam par snang ba zhes bya ba/
12a6(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i sa dang ri rdul shin du bya ba snyed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa bstan du yod pa dang ldan pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud re re zhing yang /
12a7(phal chen): bsal ba'i grangs shin du bstan pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul shin du phra bsdong dang / ldan pa bskal ba re re zhing yang bsal ba bang ma'i shin du snyan pa du ma dang ldan pa
12a8(phal chen): 'bral ba bar ma ri ni pa yang 'jig rten gyi khams rnam pa pa dang dubya ba bstan bdum dang ldan pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa 'byung ba dang / chu 'phrul sna tshogs su sun du mangs
12b1(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa 'byung bdir ning yang mang sde yang dag par bstan pa/ 'jig rten mi khams kyi rnam shin du thab sred brjod du yod pa/ mang wA rala'ang byang chub skyengs/
12b2(phal chen): da pa'i lung bstan pa 'jig rten gyi khams brjod du med pa'i rdul shin du tha bsnyed sngan du yang ba/ sems can 'dul ba mtha' dang dbus med bshin du bsen pa theg pa za dang pa'i tshum
12b3(phal chen): kyis bsgrubs pa/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa dang / cho 'phrul sna tshogs kyis rnam par 'dul ba dang ldan pa yongs su sbyangs te/ rigs kyi bu 'jig rter gyi khams
12b4(phal chen): mchog sor rin po che'i ri sro rnam par snang ba der 'jig rten gyi khams bar ma'i rgyang phyogs kun du mngon par ltas pa'i sgo rgyal mtshan gyis rnam par brgyan pa zhes bya ba byung ste/
12b5(phal chen): rigs kyi bu 'jig rten gyi khams par ma'i rgyud phyogs kun du sgo mngon par lngas brgyal mtshan gyis rnam par brgyan pa der 'jig rten gyi khams rin po che thams cad kyi mdog kun du
12b6(phal chen): snang ba'i dpal zhes bya ba 'jig rten gyi khams kyi gzhi dang / mtshams kyi rgyan rin po che'i rgyal po de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po byang chub rab du snang ba las
12b7(phal chen): byas pa/ rin po che sna tshogs kyis me tog rgya mtsho la gnas pa/ lhun rin po che'i rgyal po de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku sprul pa'i gzugs brnyan rab tu stonapa
12b8(phal chen): las bsgrubs pa/ lha'i grong khyer gyi dbyibs su 'dug pa rnam par dag cing kun nas nyon mongs pa byung bar gyur te/ 'jig rten gyi khams der gling bzhi pa'i 'jig rten
13a1(phal chen): kyi khams ri rab kyi rdul shin du phra ba steng byung bar gyur to// gling bzhi pa'i ri rab kyi rdul shin du zla ba skyed pa de dag gi gling bzhi pa dbum
13a2(phal chen): rin po chesna tshogs kyi rtse mo'i rgyal mtshan nes b+ha ba byung ste/ gling bzhi pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams rin po che sna tshigs kyi rtse mo'i rgyal mtshan der meng chu zheng dung bag
13a3(phal chen): ched brgya phrag spong yad bzhig zung nas/ gling re rar yang grong khyer chen po stong phrag re re byung ngo // gling chen po bzhi pa de'i 'dzam bu'i gling gi dbus su/ rgyal po
13a4(phal chen): gnas rin po che'i sa las rnam par brgyan pa sprin gyi sgron ma zhes bya ba grong khyer stong phrag bcu'i 'khor dang ldan pa byung ngo // de'i tshe 'dzam bu'i gling de'i mi rnams kyang
13a5(phal chen): tshe'i lce stong phrag bcu thub par gyur to// rgyal po'i gnas rin po che'i sa las rnam par brgyan pa sprin gyi sgron ma der/ 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po chos thams cad
13a6(phal chen): kyi ri'i gdugs kyi dkyil 'khor rab du sgrog pa zhes bya ba byung ste/ 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po chos thams cad kying ro'i gdugs kyi dkyil 'khor ra
13a7(phal chen): sgeg pa de'i khron po ni lnga bcu byung ngo // btsun ma ni sring zag drug byung ngo // sras ni kun kyang dpa' brtul 'ad ba/ yan+d+ra lag dam pa'i gzugs dang ldan pa/
13a8(phal chen): bltan stug pa/ gzi brjed che ba/ sdebs che ba brgya phrag bdun byung ngo // rtul po chos thams cad kying ro'i gzugs kyi dkyil 'khor rab tu sdug pa de'i rgyal
13a9(phal chen): 'jam bu'i gling thams cad gdugs gcig gis sbyangs par gyur ni/ pha rol gyi 'khor dang draka thams cad kyang shin du tshoms par gyur to// de'i tshe 'jig rten
13b1(phal chen): rmi khams dang bsal ba bar bani bang duH/ rlog pa lngani 'jig rten du byung / dge ba bcu'i las kyi yA pa ni nu ba bar gyur nas/ sems can ming ga 'acu'i mamam
13b2(phal chen): babal cher ngan song du'ang 'dong bar gyur/ de dag mi dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam yongs su 'dzin pa'i rgyus che thung ba dang / longs spyod chung ba dang / gzugs
13b3(phal chen): legs pa dang / kha dog mi sdug pa dang / lus ma legs pa dang / bde ba'i rnam bzung ba dang / sdug bsngal rnams su myong ba'i rnam pa mang ba dang / bar d+hA rgyu ning
13b4(phal chen): 'dring ba'i rang bzhin can/ bai raN+Dar dbye ba la zhugs pa dang / zhe gcod pa'i tshig la spyod pa dang / 'chal pa'i tshig tu sra ba dang / 'dod pa mi zad pas zil gyis na
13b5(phal chen): ba dang / zhe sdang ba'i yid kyis rtog pa dang ldan pa dang / lta ba'i thibs po sna tshogs kyi mya ngan du khyams par gyur nas/ de dag chos ma yin pa'i 'dod chags la zhen
13b6(phal chen): cing / 'dong ba mi zad pas zil gyis non la/ log pa'i chos kyis kun nas 'khor bas sal shing rtsi dang / lo zas skye bar 'gyur ba'i char yang dus su mi 'bab
13b7(phal chen): bar 'gyur te/ sems can de dag kyang rtswa dang gel ba dang / sman dang nags tshal dang / bza shing gi rab dang / sdong po dag kyang skams par gyur nas/ nang sa
13b8(phal chen): tshogs kyis thabs shing byags dang byigs mtshams su byabam med pas pan tshun 'amang mi kyang shing g.yen sde ba gyung / rang ga sur kyang gcig tu
14a1(phal chen): rgyal po'i gnas rin po che'i sa las rnam par brgyan pa/ sprin gyi sgron ma gang na ba der dong ste/ kun nas bskor nas la las ni lag pa snyen
14a2(phal chen): du sred/ la la ni thal mo skyong / la la ni lus shin du'angar/ la la ni myed/ la la ni brub/ la la ni lus thams cad kyis bab cing phyag 'tshal/ la la ni lam
14a3(phal chen): pus mo sa la 'jugs/ la la ni lag pa nam mkha'i dbyings su g.yo ba/ la la ni gos med cing sgren mor 'khod/ la la ni kha mig mi sdug par gyur cing / rgyal
14a4(phal chen): chos thams cad kyi nga ro'i gdugs kyi dkyil 'khor rab tu sgrogs pa la mngon du ltas shing / snying rje rje skad du'i dod chen po 'bod de/ lha chen po bdag cag ni nyam thag go/
14a5(phal chen): bkres pa dang / skom pa'i sdug bsngal gyis rab tu gzir to// 'jigs pa sna tshogs kyis dben spyo'o// bdag cag la skyabs ma mchis so// bdag cag la 'gon
14a6(phal chen): dang dpung mnan ma mchis so// sdug bsngal gyi shing brags kyis 'khor to// srog chang la thug go// 'chi bar gyur pa khang do// zhes skye sngags sna tshogs sum ning
14a7(phal chen): dbyangs kyi rnam pa sna tshogs dang / tshig sna tshogs kyis kha gdong mi sdug par gyur par 'du shes dang / tshig sna tshogs kyi tha snyad dang / tshe'i bring dang / skad kyi gdangs
14a8(phal chen): ngan ma chags brjo pa'i tshig dang / ngag gis la ring bas so// rgyal po'i gangs de'i skyes pa dang / zung med dang / rtse'u dang / bral 'akres pa dang / semangs
14b1(phal chen): man pa/ lus la rgyun med pa/ skad thogs med pa/ kha dog dang mdog mi sdug pa/ lus gas shidu drwa ba pa/ sdug bsngal zhing ying mi bde la mi dga' ba dang /
14b2(phal chen): thams cad kyang bde ba ni mngon par 'dod/ sdug bsngal gyi 'jigs pas ni bairla khyer nas/ rgyal po shes pa'i skyes bu chen mchos thams cad kying ra'i gdugs
14b3(phal chen): dkyil 'khor rab tu sgrog pa de la bde ba thams cad thob par bya ba'i 'du shes dang / sdug bsngal thams cad dang 'grogs par bya ba'i 'du shes dang / 'tshe ba'i bsam
14b4(phal chen): ba dang ldan zhing gter thob par bya ba'i 'du shes dang / mu stegs thong bar bya ba'i 'du shes dang / lam chen po la nan tan du bya ba'i 'du shes dang / grwa chen po'i
14b5(phal chen): 'du shes dang / ye shes kyi gling chen po'i 'du shes dang / don chen po rab tu thob par bya ba'i 'du shes dang / mtho ris kyi dga' ba dang / bde ba thams cad rang
14b6(phal chen): tu thob par bya ba'i 'du shes kyis mgon dang skyabs tshol bar gyur to// rgyal po chos thams cad kying ro'i gdugs kyi dkyil 'khor rab tu sgrog byas 'khor kun
14b7(phal chen): nas spang ba mang ba snying rje rje skad du 'bod pa'i 'o dong chen po de thos nas/ de snying rje chen po'i sgo brgya stong grangs med pa phrag bcu la zhugs par gyur to// de sring rje chen po'i chug
14b8(phal chen): yid la bab pa'i sems su gyur nas/ yud tsam zhig rtse gcig tu bsams te/ snying rje chen po dang ldan pa'i tshig bcu brjod do// bcu gang zhe na/ kyi hud kye sems ca
15a1(phal chen): 'di dag ni 'khor ba'i g.yangs sa chen por lhung yang skyabs med ba ldan/ bdag nam zhig 'khor ba'i g.yangs sa chen por ltung ba'i sems can/
15a2(phal chen): rnams/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sa la dgod pas gnas su 'gyur/ kyi hud kyi sems can 'di dag nyon mongs pa'i gnod pas gces shing skyabs med pa ldan/ nam zhig
15a3(phal chen): bdag sems can nyon mongs pa sna tshogs kyi 'jigs pa dang / gnod pas gces te/ skyabs med pa rnams kha nas mtho ba'i las kyi mtha' la 'god pas skyabs su 'gyur/
15a4(phal chen): kyi chung sems can 'di dag 'jig rten na rga shi'i 'jigs pas char gcod cing mgon med pa ltan/ nam zhig bdag sems can mgon med pa rnams kyi 'khor ba'i 'jigs pa thams
15a5(phal chen): can rnam par sel bas mgon du 'gyur/ kyi hud sems can 'di dag 'jig rten gyi 'jigs pa sna tshogs kyis gces te/ rten med pa lda na/ nam zhig bdag sems can gyi
15a6(phal chen): 'jigs pa sna tshogs kyis gtses pa rnams shin du bde zhing ston med pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i lam la 'god pas rten du 'gyur/ gyi hud kye ma sems can gyi 'jig rten ni ma ri//
15a7(phal chen): pa'i mun par 'joms te/ betsom dang yid gnyis kyi rang rib kyis sgribs pa ldan/ nam zhig bdag sems can thams cad kyi ma rig pa'i mun pa rnam par sel bas sman mas
15a8(phal chen): gyur ba 'ong / kyi chung sems can 'di dag ni snang ba dang bral ba ldan/ nam zhig bdag ye shes kyi sgor ba rib med pa yongs su ston pas ye shes chen po'i snang ba 'byin par
15b1(phal chen): 'gru ba byasems can 'di san dram ras dang / 'jungs pa dang / kA ma dang / sgra'i nogapas bsam bzlog pa na gyurang / bags kyi du sa
15b2(phal chen): nam zhig bdag sems can thams cad shin du dag pa la rab tu 'gad cing zan mang ba'i mo zhes kyi mang ga rab du gsal bar bying bar 'gyur/ mi thang kyi sems sa dzin te
15b3(phal chen): 'khor ba rgya bacha'i yul gyi klung du zhugs shing 'dzin pa wAn/ nam zhig bdag sems can thams cad chos rgya mtsho'i tshul la 'jud cing 'dren par 'gyur bar 'ong / kyi chung kyi mams
15b4(phal chen): can gyi 'jig rten ma dul zhing rnam par 'dren pa med pa lji na/ nam zhig bdag sems can thams cad rnam pa thams cad du yongs su srin par bya ba dang / rnam par 'dul ba la
15b5(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyi rlabs kyis dus las mi 'da' zhing rnam par 'dren par gyur par 'ong ngo // kyi hud kye sems can gyi 'jig rten ring dmus long du gyur te/ yongs su
15b6(phal chen): 'dren pa med bldan/ nam zhig bdag sems can thams cad sgrib pa med pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi tshul la 'jud cing yongs su 'dren par 'gyur/ de skad du ngas
15b7(phal chen): snying rje chen po dang ldan pa'i tshig rnam pa bcu brjod nas/ rgyal po'i gnas der dril chen po brdungs te/ gtong ba chen po'i rnga bo che yang yongs su brdungs nas/ su ci 'dod pa
15b8(phal chen): de la de sbyin gyis/ 'gro ba thams cad kyang yongs su tshim par bya'o zhes sgra brjod de/ nges 'jam bu'i gling thams cad kyi rgyal po'i gnas thams cad dang / grong dang grong byed
16a1(phal chen): dang / ljongs dang / yul dang / grong rdal thams cad du yo byad thams cad kyi mdzod bye ste/ lam gyi bzhi mdo dang / lam gyi sum mdo dang / srang tham
16a2(phal chen): cad du yang yo byad sna tshogs kyi rnam pa mang po bkod de/ 'gro ba thams cad nye bar 'tshe bar bstabs so// mdzod dang bang ba thams cad kyang bye ste/ rin po che'i gter chen po
16a3(phal chen): dang tshogs kyang yongs su bstan to// rin po che rnam pa sna tshogs kyi phung po du ma'ang srungs so// zas dang skom dang / gos dang / bzhon pa dang / me tog dang / zeng ba dang /
16a4(phal chen): bdug pa dang / byug pa dang / bye ma dang / gres rin po che kha dog sna tshogs kyi mjed bye nas/ khang pa dang / gzhal med khang dang / khyim mang po mal chu dang / stan dang /
16a5(phal chen): gos kyis yongs su brgyan te/ nor dang dbyigs thams cad phun sum tshogs par byas nas/ nor bu rin po che'i rgyal po snang ba'i gzi brjid rnam par bkod pas/ mun pa
16a6(phal chen): rnam par sel ba ba shams nas/ des sems can de dag ci 'dod pa'i bsam pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir/ khyim de dag re rerang yang rang gi lus mngon pa
16a7(phal chen): dang 'dra ba'i sprul pa'i lus mngon par sprul te/ kun du bkod do// sems can thams cad kyi nang thams cadadags pa'i phyir sman pa dang / sman dang rim gro ba dang /
16a8(phal chen): ba'i yi byang sna tshogs kyi rkyen phun sum tshogs pa yongs su bshams so// rin po che sna tshogs kyi snong rnam pa tha dang pa yiyo byang sna tshogs kyis ci rigs su bkang bar/
16b1(phal chen): rkang na par bka dang / 'di ltar rin pa che rje'i slad na sras kyinar bu rin po che sna tshogs kyis yongs su bka / smras kyi nong bu rin po ches tshogs kyi sna dza /
16b2(phal chen): kha dzag dam pasna chags kyis mongs bkang ngo // shing rnga mang po dbyibs dang / mdog sna tshogs su 'dug pa rin po chesna tshogs kyis rab tu brgyan pa/ ni dang glang 'dzad
16b3(phal chen): ba lang cang shes la byas pa rin po che'i shing rta sna tshogs rgyal po'i rkyen du rung ba/ rin po che thams cad kyi rgyan gyi longs skyong dang ldan pa/ stan sna tshogs bzhing /
16b4(phal chen): rin po chom chags kyis rnam par brgyan pa/ tha re sna tshogs bres pa/ rin po che'i dril bu'i dra ba zes pa/ gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang / 'angan bsgreng bas brgyan
16b5(phal chen): bdag gis kyang yul gyi phyogs gang bar bkod do// grong dang / grong khyer dang / ljongs dang / yul thams cad sbyin par yang 'o dad kyis sgon// brda' shing kri ba dang
16b6(phal chen): kun dga'i ra ba dang / dka' thub kyi nags tshal sna tshogs yongs su gtang ba dang / khyim dang / chung ma dang / bu dang bu mo thams cad yongs su gdang ba dang / rin po che rin
16b7(phal chen): thang med pa thams cad yongs su gtong ba dang / rang gi snying dang / rkang dang / mkhal ma dang / tshil dang / sha dang / khrag dang / pags pa dang / rka lag dang / rna ba dang /
16b8(phal chen): mig dang / sna dang / lce dang / so dang / mchu dang / mgo yongs su btang ba nas phyi nang gi dngos po thams cad rnam pa thams cad du yongs su bdang bar yang 'o dod kyis sgo'o/
17a1(phal chen): des yo byad de lta bu yongs su gtang ba'i rnam pa mang po bshams te bsogs nas/ rgyal po'i gnas rin po che'i sa las rnam par rgyad pa spyid gyi
17a2(phal chen): sgron ma de'i shar phyogs logs na grong khyer rin chen rtse mo'i gzi brjid ces bya ba'i mdun rol na/ sa bzhi mnyam pa'i phyogs yangs pa chu zheng du rgya che zhing mnyam pa mthon
17a3(phal chen): dman med pa rnam par dag cing gzhi mnam pa/ ngam grogs dang / g.yang sa dang / sdong dum dang / tsher ma dang / gseg ma dang / gyo mo thams cad med pa/ rin po che thams cad
17a4(phal chen): kyi khams las grub pa/ gzhi rin po che thams cad las byas shing rin po che'i rgyal po thams cad bkram pa/ nor bu rin po che'i rgyun rnam pa du mas brgyan pa/ rin po che'i
17a5(phal chen): me tog sna tshogs kyis gang ba/ bye ma sna tshogs dri shin du zhim pa'i rdul ldang ba/ bdug spos sna tshogs kyis bdugs pa/ rin po che'i sgron ma dpal gyi gzi brjid
17a6(phal chen): can rab tu 'bar ba/ spos dang / bdug spos thams cad kyin thun dang / smin mis nam mkha' kun du khebs pa'i rgyan dang ldan pa rin po che sna tshogs kyi shing gi zing
17a7(phal chen): ba legs par bkye bas mdzes par brgyan pa/ khang pa dang / gnal med khang dang / khang brtsegs pa sna tshogs kyis yongs su brgyan pa/ gdugs dang / rgyal
17a8(phal chen): mtshan dang / ba dan bsgreng ba/ rin po che'i rnam bu lding ba rnam par ldang ba/ rin po che sna tshogs kyi me tog gi dra bas khebyas pa/ rin po che sras thams cad kyirgyal
17b1(phal chen): ba'i dra ba'i gdugs dkyil 'a'agyu/ gsar min pa las rin tha ma la du la rnal ba dang ldan pa pacos tshogs kyis rnam pa mangs par byasang+yas skye/
17b2(phal chen): bAr bris pa/ sras kyi tshul bas chags kyi bla ma rnam par mam pa/ rin po chesna tshogs kyi me tog si lams dka' dga' lar gang ba/ rol me badrung ba dang / dkrol rgya
17b3(phal chen): khrig brgya spang gi sgra skad yid du'ang ba 'byung ba rin pa tshe thams cad kyi rgyan sna tshogs rnam par dag pas rnam par 'gyur pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i las rnam par sri rabs 'dzod
17b4(phal chen): bar grub pa zhig yong ba de'i dbus su song ge'i khri chen po rin po che sna bcu las grub pa'i sa gzhi sna tshogs la gnas pa rin po che'i khri 'bang sna tshogs bcu'i 'khor gyis rnam pa
17b5(phal chen): mdzes par byas pa/ rin ze che'i shing yal gcan bcus stegs bu'i chams sa rnam par klubs pa'i rgyan mdzes pa dang ldan pa/ rdo rje'i 'khor lo'i sa gzhi mi shigs bra la/
17b6(phal chen): rkang pa rab tu rten pa/ rin po che thams cad kyi gzugs dang / mdog yongs su 'dzin pa'i stan gyi 'khor lo can rin po che du ma las byas pa'i 'og re'i rgyan brgya phrag du mas
17b7(phal chen): brgyan pa/ rin po che sna tshogs kyi tshom bu rnam pa tha dad pa'i rgyan gyis shin du brgyan pa rin po che'i rgyal mtshan kun nas rnam par phye ste/ 'brel bar bsgreng ba/ rin po che'i
17b8(phal chen): sna chags kyi bdan sbyangs pa rnam pa pa dang pa'i rgyan dang ldan pa/ rim ma che'i dril bu'i dra bas brgyan pa'i lha rdzas kyi rin po che sna tshogs dang / gser mi dra bas tshogs
18a1(phal chen): rnam par bres pa/ rin po che sna tshogs kyi me tog gi dra ba dang / rin po che'i rgyal po chen po'i dra ba dang / gos rin po che sna tshogs dang / rin po che'i dra bas
18a2(phal chen): ci rigs su kun nas bkab cing mdzes par byas pa'i rgyan dang ldan pa/ spos rin po che rnam pa tha dad pa'i tshogs las snyim pas bcus shing spos kyi sprin mngon par gtor ba/
18a3(phal chen): rin po che'i rgyal po kha dog dang dri bsam gyis mi khyab pa las byung ba'i dbyibs yid du 'ong ba sna tshogs dang / spos thams cad kyi na bun dang / sprin 'byung ba gam yo nas lha rdzas
18a4(phal chen): kyi spos dang / bdug spos sna tshogs kyis rab tu bdugs pa/ lha rdzas las kyang 'das pa'i stan reg na bde ba kha dog bzang po du ma can legs par gting ba/ lha rdzas kyi rol
18a5(phal chen): mo dang / gru sman pa/ yid du 'ong ba brgya stong du ma'i sku kun nas 'byung ba/ rin po che'i sna tshogs kyi them skas kyis phreng ba ba dan gyis rnam par klubs pas rab tu brgyan pa'i
18a6(phal chen): rgyun dang ldan pa/ rin po che'i 'bru'i gzugs rin po che sna tshogs kyis sbas pa/ rnam par 'khrul pa sna tshogs kyis rnam par sdang bar byed pa'i 'odi dang ldan pa mngon par gyur
18a7(phal chen): ste/ de la rgyal po chos thams cad kying ro'i gdugs kyi dkyil 'khor rab tu sgrog pa gzugs bzang ba/ shin du mdzes pa/ bldan sdug pa/ kha dog bzang po dam brgyas
18a8(phal chen): ba dang ldan pa/ mi chen po'i mtshan rnam par dag pa rab tu thob pa/ rin po che rnam par sdang ba'i cong ban can/ rdo rje mthu bo che lngar 'khregs shing mi shigs pa'i lus da/
18b1(phal chen): ldan pa/ rtsi baba'i mtshams thags bzang zhing brtan par 'brel ba/ yan lag dang ni lag thams cad yangs su bzang ba/ kun nas ma sus/ gnas ldan
18b2(phal chen): ba rnam pa'i mchog thams cad dang ldan pa/ chos kyi rgyal ze chen pa'i rigs su byung ba/ ye byung thams cad la dbang rab tub pa/ chos kying zhi dzi /
18b3(phal chen): dag pa/ rang gi sems la dbang sgyur ba/ tshig gi dkyil 'khor kham bab pa/ mau khrugs pa'i ye shes dang ldan pa/ chos kyi sbyor ba ma nor ba shin du 'jan
18b4(phal chen): byas pa/ yon tan dang legs par mtha' yas par brjod du yod pa de 'dug par gyur to// rgyal po chos thams cad kyi nga ro'i gdugs kyi dkyil 'khor rab du sgrog
18b5(phal chen): deseng ga gi khri chen po la 'dug pa dang / steng gi spyi ba'i gling ka'i bar snang la gdugs kyi dkyil 'khor chen po rin po che sna chags rnam par 'phel ba'i yu ba na/
18b6(phal chen): bu rin po che dam pa'i mdzod kyi snying po dang ldan pa/ rin po che sna tshogs kyi shar bu brgya stong gis legs par bres pa/ rin po che du ma'i 'od 'phro ba/ dpal gyi gzi brjing
18b7(phal chen): rab tu 'bar bas rnam par brgyan pa/ 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser 'od 'phro zhing gsal la rnam par dag pas bla nas bkub pa/ rin po che sna tshogs sra bar spel bas
18b8(phal chen): spras pa'i gser gyi dra bas nang shun gyi rgyan byas pa/ mu tig sna tshogs kyi se mo do mngon par sbyangs pa/ rin po che sna tshogs kyi dra bas kun nas bkab pa/
18'a1(phal chen): rin po che'i dril bu'i dra ba las gser rin po che'i dril chen rin po che'i chun po'i lda ldi la rgyus pa mngon par sbyangs pa/ nor bu rin po che'i dam
18'a2(phal chen): ba'i phreng ba kun nus mngon par sbyangs pa'i rgyan dang ldan pa/ lha rdzas kyi sgra yid du 'ong ba'i gdangs grag par byung ba/ sems can thams cad dge ba'i las kyi lam
18'a3(phal chen): la skul ba'i dril gyi smanam par grag par byung bar 'gyur te/ rgyal po chos thams cad kyi nga ro'i gdugs kyi dkyil 'khor rab tu sgrog pa/ rin po che'i rdul yab
18'a4(phal chen): gyis mngon par g.yab cing / lha'i dbang po brgya byin pas kyang lhag par gzi brjid rab tu 'bar bas shin du mdzes so// de seng ge'i khri de la 'dug mthag tu 'grub
18'a5(phal chen): mang po de dag bla ngon du gyur te/ thal mo sbyar nas rgyal po de la phyag 'tshal lo// de nas rgyal po chos thams cad kyi nga ro'i gdugs kyi dkyil 'khor rab tu sgrog pa/ de'i drung /
18'a6(phal chen): du spong ba srog chags bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong sna tshogs dngos po sna tshogs yongs su len pa/ ye byang sna tshogs la mes pa/ rigs sna tshogs dang ldan pa/ 'gro ba
18'a7(phal chen): sbyang sna tshogs su gtogs pa/ 'dod pa sna tshogs kyi sems dngaldan pa/ spor ba dang bsam pas tshogs can/ phyogs sna tshogs nas 'dus bya/ yul gyi stong pa
18'a8(phal chen): tshigs la gnas pa/ longs spyod sna tshogs la mngon par smon pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ bsam pa dang yongs su rtogs pa sna tshogs can/ mi'i ris sna tshogs su
18'b1(phal chen): gzugs pa/ rigs kyi skye gnas snachags su skyes pa/ yul sna chags nas 'das pa/ sgras dang shig gi 'ang byed sna rdzogs dang lda ngas hA
18'b2(phal chen): sna tshogs 'byin pa/ dngos po sna tshogs kyi don du gsol ba 'debs pa/ tshig dang ngag sna tshogs brjod pa/ bsad dmas kyi ri rab chen po de 'brang zhig gi gdang dul
18'b3(phal chen): 'di 'ba' zhig shes pa'i skyes bu chen po yin zhes nges par sems pa bsod nams chen pos bstan pa'o// skyes bu chen po'i rtsa ba'o// gtong ba chen po'i bas ma 'ang ldan
18'b4(phal chen): ba'o// zhes bya bar 'dun pa'i sems kyis rtog pa'o// byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam gyi sems kyis 'dus pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam gyi sems kyis
18'b5(phal chen): sprul pa'i slongs mo pa'i tshogs chen po de mthong nas/ srengs me ba de dag la sems dga' ba dang / sems mos pa dang / sems spo ba dang / dge ba'i bzhes gnyen mthong
18'b6(phal chen): ba'i 'du shes su gyur to// snying rje chen po'i shugs drag po shin du yangs pa yang byung bar gyur to// mchi ma'i mtha'i skal par spongs mo pa thams cad yongs su tshim par byas
18'b7(phal chen): ba las phyir mi ldeg pa'i brtson 'grus kyis shugs drag po yang skyes par gyur to// 'gro ba thams cad du snyoms pa'i sbyor bas yongs su gtang ba'i sems kyis rgyas par
18'b8(phal chen): dgang ba'i sprin kyang mngon par 'byung bar 'gyur te/ rgyal po chos thams cad kyi nga ro'i gdugs kyi dkyil 'khor rab tu sgrog pa des slongs mo pa de dag mthong ba'i mdo la de'i
19a1(phal chen): rgyas ches dga' bar gyur mi/ bsal bas mtshams med pa'i mthas klas par stong gsum gyi 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po thob pas ni ma yinan/
19a2(phal chen): bsal ba bye ba zag khrig brgya stong mang po'i mthas klas par brgya byin gyi dbang la gnas pas ni ma yin no// bskal ba bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong mang po'i mthas klas par rab
19a3(phal chen): mtshe ma'i lha'i rgyal po'i dbang la gnas 'thob pas ni ma yin no// bskal 'bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong mang po'i mthas klas par rab dga' ldan gyi wa'i rgyal po'i dbang la gnas
19a4(phal chen): pas ni ma yin no// bsal ba tshad med pa'i mthas klas par rab 'phrul dga'i lha'i rgyal po'i dbang phyug gi dbang la gnas pa thob pas ni ma yin no// bskal pa bsam gyis mi
19a5(phal chen): khyab pa'i mthas klas par dbang sgyur gyi lha'i rgyal po'i dbang rab tu thob ste/ lha mo bzhin bzang mo yid du 'ong bas bsnyen bkur bas ni ma yin no// bskal ba brjod du med pa'i
19a6(phal chen): mthas klas par tshangs pa'i gnas kyi bde bas chang ba'i thabs la gnas pa thob pas ni ma yin no// bskal pa mtha' yas pa'i mtha' klas par gya nom snang ba'i ba'i lha'i
19a7(phal chen): bde ba thob pas ni ma yin no// bskal pa dpag tu med cing mi zad bang dge rgyas kyi lha'i bde bathob pas ni ma yin no// bskul ba ma med pa'i mabs klas par gnas gca
19a8(phal chen): khwa'i rnam par 'phrul bzhi pa'i bde ba la rnam par skying pa thobapas ni ma yin no// rigs kyi bu 'di lnga ste dper na sras bu sred pa la spyod pa ma dang / bu ru dang / bu ming das
19b1(phal chen): mnga' ba dang / zin pa dang / gnan tha zhes dang / blang sa bum dang / chung ma dang / yun ring ma nag tu zlal la// 'brag dgi bang brtsams te/ da ga du
19b2(phal chen): bra las de dag dang phrad na de dag mthong bas mi joms shing / dga' ba dang chags pa chen po skye bar 'gyur ro// rigs kyi bu de bzhin du rgyal po ches thams cad kyi tshe'i gdugs
19b3(phal chen): kyi dkyil 'khor rab tu sgrog pas slongs po pa de dag mthong bar gyur pa'i mod la dga' ba'i shugs chen po skyes so// sems kyi dga' ba'i ro bde ba dang ldan par gyur ro//
19b4(phal chen): sems sme ba'i shugs rab tu byung ngo // rab tu dga' ba chen po'i shugs yongs su skyes so// sangs rgyas kyi byang chub tu dang ba dang / mos pa'i shugs kyi stobs rkyen
19b5(phal chen): bo 'phel to// thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du dge ba'i rtsa ba brtan pa'i dad pa rnam par 'phel to// sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos la lhag pa'i bsam pa rnam par dag pa'i
19b6(phal chen): stobs mngon par 'phel to// byang chub sems dpa'i dbang po las su rung ba yongs su byung ngo // sems dga' bas rgyas par mos pa'i shugs chen po skyes par
19b7(phal chen): gyur to// sems spro ba'i shugs yangs pas dge ba'i bshes gnyen la dbang po dang bsam pa shin du gus par gyur to// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ rgyal po chos thams cad kyi
19b8(phal chen): ro'i gdugs kyi dkyil 'khor rab tu sgrog pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du dmigs pa la brtson pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la rab tu gzhol ba/ thams cad mkhyen pa
20a1(phal chen): nyid kyi las dang / sgol mngon du ltas pa/ 'gro ba thams cad shin du tshim par bya ba'i yid la bya ba la brtson pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad
20a2(phal chen): gyi yon tan rgya mtsho la 'jug pa'i nan tan la 'dun pa dang / bdud dang / las dang nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa thams cad kyi ri rnam par 'thor ba la brtson pa/ de bzhin gshen
20a3(phal chen): pa thams cad kyi gdams ngag 'thun par grang ba la sta gon du gnas pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba rgya mtsho sgo kun nas/ yongs su bsdu ba la brtson pa'i snying po can/ mngon par
20a4(phal chen): zhen pa thams cad las gyen du 'phags pa'i rgyu dang ldan pa/ 'jig rten gyi yul thams cad la mngon par zhen pa med pa/ chos kyi rang bzhin nam mkha'i spyod yul can
20a5(phal chen): des slongs mo pa de dag la bu cig pa'i 'du shes bskyed pa'i phyir ro// ba dang ma'i 'du shes dang / sbyin pa'i gnas kyi 'du shes dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi 'du shes
20a6(phal chen): dang / dgon pa'i 'du shes dang / dka' ba byed pa'i 'du shes dang / mang po byas pa'i 'du shes dang / phan 'dogs pa dam pa'i 'du shes dang / byang chub kyi la mnye ba
20a7(phal chen): ston pa'i 'du shes dang / mkhan pa'i 'du shes dang / smon pa'i 'du shes bsred pa'i phyir te/ de ltar des spongs ma pa de dag ni cil 'das pa dang / don cil byin pa/
20a8(phal chen): dngu/ dus ci tsam nas 'dus pa dang / yul gang dang gdan gnas pa dang / dngos po cidang ci spong ba dang / rnam pa gang 'dong ba dang / bsam bci'adra ba dang /
20b1(phal chen): la smon pa dang / ci dang ci 'dong ba dang / dngas pa gang dang gang tshol ba de dag thams cad tshul bzhin du mi dga' ba med pa'i byams brten pa'i dkyil 'byung dang / blangamazang
20b2(phal chen): 'gro ba las byin phyogs su ma ltas pa'i gtong ba chen po 'du gzer dang / sems can thams cad la snyoms par sbyor ba'i gdong ba'i sgras yongs su rim par byas so// nges
20b3(phal chen): zas 'dod pa la ni zas sbyin no// skom 'dong pa la ni skom byin no// gos 'dong ba la ni gos byin no// me tog 'ding ba la ni me tog byin no// de bzhin du sras dang / phreng ba
20b4(phal chen): dang / byug pa dang / phye mo dang / gos dang / gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan dang / rin po che dang / rgyan dang / stan dang / mal dang / khyim dang gzhal med khang dang / btsu

20b6(phal chen): bzhon pa dang / gser dang / dbyig dang / nor bu dang / mu tig dang / dung dang / mal shel dang / byi ru dang / sa le sbram dang / dngul dag kyang byin par gyur to// rang gi khyim dang /

20b8(phal chen): de khyer cig ces nas yul 'dod pa dag kyang yul byin no// grong 'dod pa dag kyang grong byin no// grong khyer 'dod pa dag kyang grong khyer byin no// sems can thams cad la
21a1(phal chen): sgoms par zhugs pa des slongs ma pa de dag thams cad la ci bdog pa yongs su btang ste/ dngos pa thams cad yongs su btang bas mngon par

21a3(phal chen): bzang zhing mdzes la blta na sdug pa/ kha dog bzang po'i dam pa rgyas pa dang ldan pa/ mdog gser gyi kha dog lta bu dang ldan pa/ skra mthen mthing du 'dug pa/ m-i

21a6(phal chen): zab pa/ chos thang ba dang gzung ba dang / khong du chung bar bya ba la yid gzungs pa dang ldan pa/ sngon dge ba'i rna ba la legs par byas pa/ chos kyis mngon par

21a8(phal chen): ldan pa/ sangs rgyas lba ba'i phyogs la rnam par ldas pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la mngon par 'dun pa zhig mchod sbyin gyi rab chen po der 'angs te/ tshang na
21b1(phal chen): mnan na 'a sa grub brnam thams kyang ma'i gzugs kya kyil na du 'dum pa'i sa dzin ba 'grums ral
21b2(phal chen): 'dug 'dug ste/ rgyal ba de la phyag 'tshal las/ bar ci la'ang len pa med do// de phyogs gcig na 'dug cing / sems 'di ltar skyed par gyur te/ bdag gi ma
21b3(phal chen): bshes gnon 'di lta bu mthong zhing / 'grogs su yod pa ni bdag gis thob par bya ba legs par thob bo// snum ste/ des rgyal po chos thams cad byung po'i gdu
21b4(phal chen): kyi dkyil 'khor rab tu sgrog pa de la dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi 'du shes dang / ston ba'i 'du shes dang / snying brje bar byung ba'i 'du shes dang / phan 'jigs pa'i
21b5(phal chen): shes dang / sangs rgyas kyi 'du shes bskyed de/ g.yo sgyu med pa'i sems kyis dga' ba dang / mes pa dang / spro ba'i shugs rab tu yangs pa thob pas rang gi rgyur rna
21b6(phal chen): lus las bkrol te/ rgyal po chos thams cad kyi nga ro'i gdugs kyi dkyil 'khor rab tu sgrog pa gang na bder mngon par ltas te gtor ba dang / de dag de'i seng ge'i
21b7(phal chen): khri'i 'og khri 'bang gi sa'i steng du gram par gyur to// des rgyan de dag de ltar gtor nas smon lam btab pa/ 'i ldang rgyal po chos thams cad kyi nga ro'i gdugs kyi dkyil
22a1(phal chen): rab tu sgrog pa 'di sems can mgon med cing mun pa'i nang na/ 'dzem pa rnams kyi mgon skyabs su gyur pa/ de ltar bdag kyang ma 'ongs pa'i
22a2(phal chen): dus na 'gyur bar shog shig/ 'dis chos gang shes pa de dag kyang bdag gis shes par shog shig/ 'di theg pa gang gis 'byung ba des bdag kyang 'byung bar shog shig
22a3(phal chen): 'di lam gang nas zhugs pa de nas bdag kyang zhugs par sheg shig/ ji ltar 'di gzugs bldan gtang mi bral zang mi shes pa'i longs spyod dang ldan te/ g.yog 'khor
22a4(phal chen): mtha' yas la gzhan gyis mi thub cing thub par dka' ste/ thub pa med pa de bzhin bdag kyang shog shig/ 'di gang dang gang du skye bar 'gyur ba de dang der bdag kyang skye bar

29a4(phal chen): mtsho thams cad yongs su gnon pa'i thabs la mkhas pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rgya mtsho thams cad spyod pa re rer yang dag par 'dra ba'i smon lam dang stong pa
29a5(phal chen): yongs su dag pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa re re la byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa rgya mtsho thams cad yongs su 'du bar rnam par spyad pa la dbang sgyu
29a6(phal chen): bde dag gi spyod pa shes pa 'am/ yon tan brjod par nus re kan// song rigs kyi bu byang chub kyi snying po 'di nyid na/ mtshan mo'i lha mo 'gro ba thams cad bsrung ba
29a7(phal chen): sngon lam la btsun pa'i 'od ces bya ba zhig bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar byin cing 'jug gis de'i gan du song la'i ltang byang chub sems dpas blan med pa yang dag par rdzo
29a8(phal chen): ba'i byang chub tu sems can yangs su smin par bya ba dang / 'i war sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad yongs su srung bar bya ba dang / ji sa de bzhi na gshegs pa thams cad
29b1(phal chen): du sa pa rgyas byas pasnyen pag su gyur bya ba dang / lkung byung chu ba sems dbus sangs rgyas byargyas pams nga sa gyu
29b2(phal chen): de nas rlung nga ban gyi bu nor bzangs kyi sa mtshan ma'i rnam shing thams cad gyi mi dge rgyas pas bde bar gnas rlung ba gnyis la zas phyag 'dum
29b3(phal chen): lhamo zhing thams cad kyi me tog rgyas pas bde bar gnas pa la lan brgya snong du mar g.yas phyogs su sbyor ba byas nas yang dang yang du bltas te/ mtshan pa'i
29b4(phal chen): bri zhing thams cad kyi ma dog rgyas pas bde bar gnas pa'i drung nas snang ngo // de nas tshong dben gyi bu ne bzangs mtshan mo'i lA m+bu m+b+hi ba rnams ca bsdu
29b5(phal chen): smon lalal btsun pa'i 'od gangan ba der seng song nas/ mtshan mo'i ldu ma 'gro ba thams cad bsrung ba'i smon lam la 'byor ba'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor de nyid na
29b6(phal chen): ris kyi dbyings kyi tshul rab tu snang ba'i rin po che'i dra bas kun nas yog pa'i lus dang ldan pa/ nyi zla dang / gza' skar dang / rgyu skar thams cad kyi gzugs parna
29b7(phal chen): yongs su ston pa'i lus dang ldan pa/ bsam pa'i lta ba bzhin du sems can gyis rnam par dmigs par ston pa'i lus dang ldan pa/ sems can thams cad kyi lu

29b9(phal chen): rnam par dmigs par byed pa'i lus

30a3(phal chen): la mngon du gnas pa'i lus dang ldan pa/ dus thams cad du 'gro ba thams cad kyi don la mngon du ltas par nam mkha'i dbyings kyis kri ba'i lus dang ldan pa/
30a4(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi zhabs la 'dud cing phyag 'tshal ba'i lus dang ldan pa/ sems can thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba brtsegs pa la gces shing
30a5(phal chen): sngon du 'gro ba'i lus dang ldan pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad las mngon du chos kyi sprin yang dag par len cing yongs su 'dzin pa'i smon lam grub cing
30a6(phal chen): yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i sems las phyin phyogs sum gyur cing / dran pas yongs su 'dzin pa'i lus dang ldan pa/ mtha' dang dbus med pa'i 'od kyis
30a7(phal chen): thugs dang phyogs mtshams thams cad rgyas par 'grengs pa'i lus dang ldan pa/ 'dra ba thams cad kyi mun pa rnam par sel ba'i chos kyi sman ma'i 'od ldams
30a8(phal chen): 'gyed cing snang ba yongs su ston pa'i lus dang ldan pa/ chos sgyu ma'i rnam pa lnga bu'i ye shes kyi lus dri ma mang ba rab tu ston pa'i lus dang ldan pa/ chos kyi lus
30b1(phal chen): sbyin pa dang rdul du thal ba rab du sman pa'i lus dang ldan pa/ chos ning sgyu ma lnga bu las byung ba'i lus dang ldan pa/ rgyas ning rab zhunags pas su na
30b2(phal chen): sems dang ldan po/ ye shes kyi sna bas kun du gsal ba/ rag thob bzhin du na med cing gdung ba med pa'i yid kyi lus dang ldan pa/ sa
30b3(phal chen): shigs shing brtan pa dang ldan pa'i dbyings las byung ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyi rlabs gnas pa med pa'i rang ba'i dkun nas non mongs
30b4(phal chen): nga'i chos nyid kyi lus rnam par dag pa'i lus dang ldan pa de rin po che'i rgyal po 'grob thams cad kyi gnas rab du snang ba'i snying ba can gyi stan la 'dag pa dun
30b5(phal chen): nga des de mthong nas spyi bos bdud de mthong bar bya ba'i tshu la sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul shin du phra ba steng rjes su dran par byas nas sa'i gzhi las bdung
30b6(phal chen): / rnangs bcad bzhig tu mngon par bdud do// de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs sa'i gzhi de las langs de thal me sbyar nas/ mtshan mo'i lha mo'i
30b7(phal chen): ba thams cad bsrung ba'i smon lam la brtson pa'i 'od de'i lus la bltas pa dang / 'du shes rnam par dag pa bcu thob par gyur te/ de dag thob nas dge ba'i
30b8(phal chen): za shes gnyen thams cad dang skal ba mnyam par rab tu thob par gyur to// bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lnga ste/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid brtsams pa'i brtson 'grus
31a1(phal chen): la dmigs pa thams cad du gnas par bya ba'i phyir dge ba'i bshes gnyen rnams la rang gyi sems kyi 'du shes rab tu thob par gyur to//
31a2(phal chen): dge ba'i bshes gnyen bkur zhing dge ba'i rtsa ba yangs pa yongs su bsgrub pa grub par bya ba'i phyir rang gi las rnam par smin par rnam par dag pa'i rang bzhin gyi 'dra
31a3(phal chen): shes rab tu thob bo// smon lam thams cad kyis brgyan pa'i skyed pa la yang dag par gnas par bya ba'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i rgyan gyi 'du shes
31a4(phal chen): rab tu thob bo// dge ba'i bshes gnyen thams cad kyi gdams ngag gi lam land dan du bya ba'i bur sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad rab du bsgrub pa'i 'bruzhes
31a5(phal chen): rab tu thob bo// sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yul du myur ba'i chos bla na med pa la rnam par sbyong ba'i snang ba yongs su mthong bar bya ba'i phying rnams su myong ba skyed pa'i 'du shes
31a6(phal chen): rab tu thob bo// kun du bzang ba'i spyod pas byung ba'i smon lam dang / spyod pa rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir 'byung ba gcig gi 'du shes rab tu thob par gyur to// dge
31a7(phal chen): ba'i chos yongs su brtsegs pa thams cad rnam par 'phel bar bya ba'i byor thams cad mkhyen pa'i bsod nams rgya mtsho'i 'byung gnas kyi 'du shes rab tu thoba'o//
31a8(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi byang chub tu thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la brtson 'grus kyi shugs yongs su 'phel bar bya ba'i phyir dge ba'i chos yongs su ma rdzogs pa yongs sa
31b1(phal chen): ga par byed pa dang / yang drug pa phrul byar byed pa dang / gangs su snang ba'i 'du zhes rabatu byu // sems can 'asus sa
31b2(phal chen): cing mangs su rdzogs par bya ba'i byer/ dge ba'i rna ba thams cad yangs su rdzogs pa'i 'du shes rab thubab par byu na// byang chub sems
31b3(phal chen): ma dbang sgyur bar rab tu gnas bor bya ba'i phyir dge ba'i bshes gnyen rnams la don thams cad yongs su sgrub pa'i 'dun sa rab du babs/ 'dzin pa
31b4(phal chen): dag pa ban po de dag rab tu thob par gyur to// de dag thob pas mtshan mo'i lha me 'gro ba thams cad bsrung ba'i smon lam la brtson pa'i 'od snang ba las/ zung chu
31b5(phal chen): sems dpa' dang skal ba 'thun pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul shin du zla ba skyed thob par gyur te/ 'di ltar phyogs bcu'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dus gas
31b6(phal chen): rjes su dran pa'i tshul la dran pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / chos rgya mtsho'i tshul thams cad badrang bar khong du chud bar bya ba la the gros kyi skal ba mnam pa dang
31b7(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor lo'i dkyil 'khor rig pas rjes su shes par bya ba'i bye brag dang / tshul tha dad bar mkhas pa la rig pa'i skal ba
31b8(phal chen): mnaza ba dang / blo nam mkha' dang mnyam pas dus gsum thams cad kyi tshul rgya mtsho sde ba rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir/ tho'i skal ba mnyam pa dang / byang chub
32a1(phal chen): sems dpa' thams cad kyi dbang po rgya mtsho shes pa'i snang ba rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir// dbang po rnam par dag pa'i skal ba mnyam pa
32a2(phal chen): dang / rnam pa thams cad du sems can yongs su bsdu ba'i rgyan gyis rnam par brgyan pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i lam gyi yon tan la nan tan du bya ba'i rgyan gyis lam
32a3(phal chen): khong du chung bar bya ba'i phyir/ sems rnam par dag pa'i skal ba mnyam pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi spyod yul snang ba rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir stong yul
32a4(phal chen): gyi skal ba mnyam pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i tshul rgya mtsho la 'jug pa'i lam snang ba rnam pa thams cad rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir tshul gyi rjes su 'brang ba'i skal ba man
32a5(phal chen): ba dang / chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin shes shing khong du chung ba rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir don khong du chud pa'i skal ba mnyam pa dang / chos kyi tshul rgya mtsho thams cad la chos
32a6(phal chen): la rnam par spyod pa'i skal ba mnyam pa dang / sgrib pa thams cad kyi ri rnam par gtor ba'i phyir mi 'jigs pa'i skal ba mnyam pa dang / bsam pa ji la ba bzhin du 'gro ba rnam
32a7(phal chen): la rnam paza da par yongs su bstan pa'i mtshan dang dpe byad bzang pos rnam par bris pa'i lus rnam par dag par ba tu thebab bya ba'i phyir/ gzugs kyi lhas rnam pa
32a8(phal chen): dag pa'i sel ba mnyam pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' skabs yongs su rdzogs pas thams cad mkhyen pa zhid du dmigs pa rnam par 'phel bar bya ba'i phyir/ gangs
32b1(phal chen): pa sa ma dang / sems dang bams pa nas k+Sha sangs su dag par byu byung ba 'jigs pa'i gal nas 'ang/ 'phrul ba
32b2(phal chen): dpa'i spang bu la gnas pas mismra par btun pa par bya ba'i phyir bcan 'grus kyi bsol pa mnam pa dang / rnas bams pa la sgrub pa med pa'i sa skyes shA na rje
32b3(phal chen): bar bya ba'i phyir sras pa'i sprul pa mtsham pa dang / 'tsho ba thams cad la mngon par 'phags pa'i lus yongs su dag par bya ba'i b+h+ring ril zas menan po'i thams
32b4(phal chen): munam pa dang / 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad mngon par dga' bar bya ba'i tshig yongs su dag par bya ba'i phyir/ mnam bi dma'i sel ba mnam pa dang
32b5(phal chen): kyi tshul rgya mtsho thams cad kyi sgra rab du bsgrag pa'i phyir dbyangs kyi bskal ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi tshig rnam par dmigs pa'i tha snyad dang / tshul rgya mtshol
32b6(phal chen): dbyangs kyi yan lag rnam par dag pa'i bskal ba mnyam pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdams ngag gi yon tan khong du chud ba rnam par dag par bya ba la yon tan
32b7(phal chen): rnam par dag pa'i skal ba mnam pa dang / kha na ma tho ba med pa'i las rnam par smin pa yongs su dag par bya ba'i phyir chos dang las kyi rgyud du mi 'gal ba'i skal ba mangs
32b8(phal chen): pa dang / sangs rgyas byung ba thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor ba'i phyir mchod sbyin gyis chos bzang po la rab du gnas pa'i skal ba mnyam pa dang /

33a5(phal chen): mnyam pa dang / chos thams cad brjod cing sres pa la ngag gi las rnam par dag pa'i skal ba mnyam pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi sems la thams cad
33a6(phal chen): mkhyen pa nyid du dmigs pa nye bar sgrub pa'i phyir yid kyi las kyi skal ba mnyam pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad la rgyan rnam pa sna tshogs thams cad kyis
